Magic Origins RTPQ Taipei
=========================



 Posted in [ARCHIVES](/en/articles/archive)
 on July 10, 2015 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/wizards_authorpic_larger.jpg)
By Wizards of the Coast










* [Pro Tour *Battle for Zendikar* Regional Pro Tour Qualifier Top 8 Decklists](http://magic.wizards.com/en/articles/organized-play/the-pro-tour-main-stage-2015-07-10)


Thanks to [Fantasy Card Shop](https://www.facebook.com/pages/%E5%B9%BB%E6%83%B3%E9%81%8A%E6%88%B2%E4%B8%96%E7%95%8C/122740911113930?ref=bookmarks) for organizing this Regional Pro Tour Qualifier and submitting Top 8 decklists!
